# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Claude Sonnet 4 Thinking 16K

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=8.6)
    The storytelling effectively builds tension toward the midnight climax while exploring themes of liminality, academic persecution, and the boundaries between days/worlds. The metaphor of souls casting shadows across time boundaries is particularly evocative. The story skillfully shows rather than tells, with strong imagery and purposeful dialogue. While the stakes are clear, the emotional impact could be even stronger with more interior character development.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=8.0)

While the theme of forgiveness resonates, it occasionally veers toward stating emotional revelations directly rather than allowing them to emerge more subtly through action.
